<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&nbsp;8, 2020, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the
fiscal quarter ended November&nbsp;30, 2019 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed
&#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by
reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> in such a filing.
</P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

the fiscal quarter ended November&nbsp;30, 2019 and related matters. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the conference call are

highlights, year-over-year </I></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Strategic updates announced after end of quarter </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">WBA agreed to create German wholesale joint venture with McKesson </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Kroger and Walgreens formed group purchasing organization </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., January&nbsp;8, 2020 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2020, which ended
November&nbsp;30, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Executive Vice Chairman and CEO Stefano Pessina said, &#147;We are maintaining our outlook for the year despite a soft first quarter. We
are confident our strategic plans are the right ones to drive long-term sustainable growth going forward. In addition, during the quarter we were very satisfied with the progress made in our Transformational Cost Management Program and with the
strong cash flow we delivered.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of First Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Fiscal 2020 first quarter net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance decreased 24.8&nbsp;percent to $845&nbsp;million compared with the same quarter a year
ago, while net earnings per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> decreased 19.8&nbsp;percent to $0.95 compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Adjusted net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 11.8&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion,
down 11.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted earnings per share were $1.37, a decrease of 6.0&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis and a decrease of 5.7&nbsp;percent on a constant
currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sales in the first quarter were $34.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 1.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and an increase of 2.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Compared to the same quarter a year ago, operating income was $1.0&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 27.6&nbsp;percent, and
adjusted operating income was $1.5&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 15.6&nbsp;percent, down 15.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, including more than 5 percentage points of adverse items such as year-over-year bonus changes. Operating income
also reflected costs related to the acquisition of Rite Aid stores and to the implementation of the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by
operating activities was $1.1&nbsp;billion in the first quarter, an increase of $601&nbsp;million from the same quarter last year, and free cash flow was $674&nbsp;million, an increase of $684&nbsp;million from the same quarter a year earlier,
reflecting working capital efficiencies as the company executed against optimization initiatives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Company Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company maintained guidance of roughly flat growth in fiscal 2020 adjusted earnings per share at constant currency rates, with a range of plus or minus
3&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Progress on Strategic Priorities </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">During the first
quarter of fiscal 2020, and since the close of the quarter, the company made substantial progress on its four strategic priorities: accelerating digitalization; transforming and restructuring retail offering; creating neighborhood health
destinations; and the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selected highlights include the following: </P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">WBA and McKesson announced an agreement to create a German joint venture, combining their wholesale operations to drive
long term value in a key European market; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Walgreens and Kroger formed a group purchasing organization, expanding their collaboration with a new joint venture aimed
at delivering cost savings and other benefits across owned brand sourcing; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Flagship No7 beauty brand saw sales growth in the mid teens in the U.S.; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The first two of five VillageMD primary care clinics, Village Medical at Walgreens, opened in Houston;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Boots UK announced an exclusive franchise agreement in the UK with Mothercare. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Divisions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Retail Pharmacy USA</B>: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail Pharmacy USA had first quarter sales of $26.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 1.6&nbsp;percent over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter.
Sales in comparable stores increased by the same percentage. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales increased 2.9&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting higher brand inflation and prescription volume, and strong growth in central specialty. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 2.5&nbsp;percent. The division filled 294.0&nbsp;million
prescriptions, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents in the quarter, an increase of 1.4&nbsp;percent over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Prescriptions filled in
comparable stores increased 2.8&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The division&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> adjusted basis in the first quarter decreased approximately 55 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 20.9&nbsp;percent, which was in line with the fourth quarter of
fiscal 2019, as reported by IQVIA.<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> The year-over-year change includes the impact of the store optimization program. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales decreased 2.2&nbsp;percent in the first quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Comparable retail sales were
down 0.5&nbsp;percent in the quarter, mostly due to continued <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">de-emphasis</FONT> of tobacco. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> comparable retail sales increased around
0.8&nbsp;percent, reflecting solid growth in the core health and wellness and beauty categories. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">2 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 5.2&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago and adjusted gross profit decreased
4.9&nbsp;percent, with procurement savings and pharmacy prescription growth insufficient to offset <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> reimbursement pressure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">First quarter selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) as a percentage of sales decreased by 0.3 percentage point compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales decreased by 0.6 percentage point in the same period. Both decreases reflect strong cost savings, which more than offset incremental investments, impact
of inflation and higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus impact. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the first
quarter decreased 27.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $848&nbsp;million. Excluding costs related to the acquisition of Rite Aid stores and to the Transformational Cost Management Program, adjusted
operating income in the first quarter decreased 16.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $1.2&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Retail
Pharmacy International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail Pharmacy International had first quarter sales of $2.7&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 5.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting an adverse currency impact of 2.7&nbsp;percent. Sales decreased 2.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to lower retail sales in Boots UK and lower sales in Chile,
reflecting social unrest. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Comparable pharmacy sales increased 0.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, primarily due to the UK, driven by higher National
Health Service (NHS) reimbursement and increased sales of services, partially offset by lower prescription volume. Comparable retail sales decreased 3.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with Boots UK holding share in a declining market.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 6.3&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including an adverse currency impact of 2.6&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency
basis, gross profit and adjusted gross profit decreased 3.7&nbsp;percent and 3.6&nbsp;percent, respectively, reflecting lower retail sales and margin in Boots UK. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales increased 0.7 percentage point and adjusted SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales, on a constant currency basis, increased 1.3 percentage
points, both reflecting higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus impact and technology investments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the first quarter decreased 43.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $44&nbsp;million, while adjusted
operating income decreased 40.5&nbsp;percent to $79&nbsp;million, down 39.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Pharmaceutical Wholesale: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmaceutical Wholesale had first quarter sales of $6.0&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter,
including an adverse currency impact of 3.0&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, comparable sales increased 8.3&nbsp;percent, led by emerging markets and the UK, including a customer contract change in the UK. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the first quarter was $122&nbsp;million, which included $13&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. This compared
with operating income of $155&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which included $39&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Adjusted operating income increased 4.1&nbsp;percent to $229&nbsp;million, up 4.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong revenue growth and higher
contribution from AmerisourceBergen. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Dividends Declared </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">During the
first quarter, the company declared a quarterly dividend of 45.75 cents per share, unchanged from the previous quarter and an increase of 4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. The dividend was payable
December&nbsp;12, 2019 to stockholders of record as of November&nbsp;18, 2019. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">3 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through dispensing and distributing
medicines, its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The company has more than 100 years of trusted health care heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical wholesaling. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Including equity method investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 440,000 people and has more than 18,750 stores. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA&#146;s purpose is to help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy
planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. The company&#146;s businesses have been recognized for their Corporate Social Responsibility. Walgreens was named to FORTUNE* magazine&#146;s 2019 Companies that Change the World list and
Boots UK was recognized as Responsible Business of the Year 2019-2020 by Business in the Community. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2019 list of the World&#146;s
Most Admired Companies, ranked first in the food and drugstore category. This is the 26th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company, Walgreen Co., has been named to the list. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More company information is available at <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL">*&copy; 2019, Fortune Media IP Limited.&nbsp;Used under license. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under&nbsp;SEC&nbsp;rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and
presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in&nbsp;the United States&nbsp;(GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not
calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s financial
results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believe that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional
perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating
current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States
reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions,
comparable stores are defined as those that have been open for at least twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past twelve months.
Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for the first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable stores for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is
later. Comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales refer to total sales, pharmacy sales and retail sales, respectively, in such stores. For the Retail Pharmacy USA division, comparable numbers of prescriptions refer
to number of prescriptions in such stores. For the Pharmaceutical Wholesale division, comparable sales are defined as sales excluding acquisitions and dispositions. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a
result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">10 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the Retail Pharmacy Internal division, comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and
comparable retail sales, and with respect to the Pharmaceutical Wholesale division, comparable sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Refer to the discussion
above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">11 </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Beginning in the quarter ended May&nbsp;31, 2019, management reviewed and refined its practice to reflect the
proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in order
to provide investors with a comparable view of performance across periods. These adjustments include acquisition-related amortization and acquisition-related costs and were immaterial for the prior periods presented. Although the Company may have
shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their
operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;# </P>
